  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_50a33a59-8c65-42b2-9ca6-b66d4c39cf17'
      });

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer203686422" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11379752077755503389">This was my fav book for a long time. It`s still in my top five. And not just because of the style it is written in, but the way emotions are conveyed - in a subtle, yet strong manner. I especially loved Connor, because he understands human nature. He understands a person`s mind, how someone`s heart and psyche works and Guillaume gave us some of the best lines in the book through Connor. The plot is simply incredible. I read the book in six hours and then I read it again and again. And I would r</span>
  <span id="freeText11379752077755503389" style="display:none">This was my fav book for a long time. It`s still in my top five. And not just because of the style it is written in, but the way emotions are conveyed - in a subtle, yet strong manner. I especially loved Connor, because he understands human nature. He understands a person`s mind, how someone`s heart and psyche works and Guillaume gave us some of the best lines in the book through Connor. The plot is simply incredible. I read the book in six hours and then I read it again and again. And I would read it a million times more, because everytime I do I feel like I`m entering a secret, forbidden world made up of raw emotions, powerful bursts of energy and love and equally harrowing pain. I was initially put off, before I started reading, because I thought it was a chick lit, but it proved to be so much more. I strongly recommend this book to everyone who enjoys a good story with a meaning and a terrific ending, regardless of your genre preference.</span>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zahraa Maytham" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zahraa Maytham" href="/user/show/39374096-zahraa-maytham">Zahraa Maytham</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2802403243" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4492796470749697607">Like every other Guillaume Musso book that I’ve read (and this is the fifth one), it starts out perfectly and goes down the hill near the end. <br/>It’s a real page-turner, you cannot help but continue reading to know what will happen next (even though you know it will probably disappoint you). It has a great character development, so many plot twists, the author tries to keep everything connected but than the ending comes and it always brings you back to reality, and you realize that none of what yo</span>
  <span id="freeText4492796470749697607" style="display:none">Like every other Guillaume Musso book that I’ve read (and this is the fifth one), it starts out perfectly and goes down the hill near the end. <br />It’s a real page-turner, you cannot help but continue reading to know what will happen next (even though you know it will probably disappoint you). It has a great character development, so many plot twists, the author tries to keep everything connected but than the ending comes and it always brings you back to reality, and you realize that none of what you read was true. <br />Also, I don’t know if it is the translated version or the original book, but all of his books have so many mistakes, regarding names, places and even memories. <br />Still, it’s good for a fast read, just don’t get your hopes up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4492796470749697607" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_992948921" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/992948921" />
    <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines"><img alt="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466111136p2/30004027.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/992948921?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–" href="/user/show/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines">Laurie –Read Between The Skylines–</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30004027-laurie-read-between-the-skylines?shelf=read-in-french">read-in-french</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer992948921" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7432334845636844843">I have to say that I don't usually enjoy reading Musso's books. The characters are stereotypical, empty and look like each other from one book to one other (successful business man, rich, and so on... Maybe he should stop projecting what his dream life is on his character, they would probably sound more... Human).<br/><br/>Nonetheless, I have to say I really liked this book. The characters were deeper, strong and weak at the same time, and full of hope. I especially loved the ending.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3374231786" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3374231786" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4644065826133347444">This is a difficult one... it’s a confusing book that only reveals its plot at the very end with a stupefying twist. I enjoyed reading this novel and was entertained by it even though I wasn’t sure what was going on 90% of the time!<br/>The characters are slightly flat but all have interesting back stories and an intriguing connection. I would recommend this book to readers who love a good plot twist.<br/><br/>Celui-ci est difficile... je trouvais ce livre stupéfiant car il ne révèle sa vraie historie qu’à la </span>
  <span id="freeText4644065826133347444" style="display:none">This is a difficult one... it’s a confusing book that only reveals its plot at the very end with a stupefying twist. I enjoyed reading this novel and was entertained by it even though I wasn’t sure what was going on 90% of the time!<br />The characters are slightly flat but all have interesting back stories and an intriguing connection. I would recommend this book to readers who love a good plot twist.<br /><br />Celui-ci est difficile... je trouvais ce livre stupéfiant car il ne révèle sa vraie historie qu’à la fin. J’ai aimé lire ce bouquin, il m’a bien distrait même si je ne l’ai pas complètement compris la plupart du temps!<br />Les protagonistes sont un peu plats mais ils ont des histoires personelles intéressantes et un lien fascinant entre eux. Je conseille ce livre à ceux qui aiment une bonne péripétie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4644065826133347444" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1757608621" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2434681223970790288">This is my first Guillaume Musso book. I've heard a lot of people praising the author so I bought this book. It was amazing to read this story. It's filled with all kinds of emotions and it was impossible to predict what will happen next. I really appreciate that because I tend to create scenarios in my head while reading and I rarely end up surprised. I'm so glad I was surprised by this book. It was beautifully written and the title really makes sense. The love and pain all those characters fel</span>
  <span id="freeText2434681223970790288" style="display:none">This is my first Guillaume Musso book. I've heard a lot of people praising the author so I bought this book. It was amazing to read this story. It's filled with all kinds of emotions and it was impossible to predict what will happen next. I really appreciate that because I tend to create scenarios in my head while reading and I rarely end up surprised. I'm so glad I was surprised by this book. It was beautifully written and the title really makes sense. The love and pain all those characters felt really affected me. There were many tears shed but I was happy to see such immense amount of love between the characters and the healing power of it. I'll definitely read more Musso's books in the future.</span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EJoiiAkZb1pSVI0+PpIxZobQ4laUUMT+sin/Pzio0TUiFn4fbFSy7I8BMIo8rAt/S1BWhW/VSq5K1eQ7RvlG8Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zo60wIKkX8qI/HRVV0syMxR4TEZWsAbYdyVwdo2K/R38AuhX5+mCfFWpyeFVdQgq2fj4la01iIiP2Wty89tq2Q==')})
  }
//]]>

دفعة واحدة من السّماد في ربيع كلّ عام، وتربة رطبة دون فيض من السقيا.\nجميع أنواع الياسمين تفضل النّموّ في مكان مشمس، لكنّها تتحمّل وجود شيء من الظلّ. وشمس تونس كانت مواتية لنضجها وتكوين شخصيّتها، وقد أصبحت جاهزة لتحمّل شيء من ظلالأوروبا ذات المناخ البارد. مثل الياسمين الأبيض المتوسّطي، كانت رقيقة في مظهرها، لكنّ شخصيّتها قويّة وثابتة، مثل رائحة الياسمين النفّاذة والفريدة التي تبثّ إحساسا بالدّفء لا تملكه الورود الأخرى.\nلم تتكلّم عن دلالة الياسمين العاطفيّة التي بحثت ياسمين عنها مذ اهتمّت بمدلولات الزهور في بداية مراهقتها. عرفت أنّ إهداء زهر الياسمين لامرأة يعني “لماذا لا تحبّين أبدًا؟”. والدها أهداها هي، ياسمين، إلى والدتها. كانت آخر عطاياه لها حين تخلّى عن حضانتها إثر الطّلاق. وهي “لم تحبّ بعده أبدًا”. كانت جديرة بتقبّل زهرة الياسمين.\nتفتقد أمها كل يوم أكثر من اليوم الماضي. مع مرور الوقت تزداد يقينًا من ضياعها بدونها. كانت تعلم أن الغربة ليست تجربة سهلة، ومع ذلك وافقت على سفرها. علّمتها كيف تكون ياسمينة حقيقيّة. لكن لعلّها غفلت عن حقيقة مرّة. زهرة الياسمين تذبل بسرعة حين تغادر تربتها وتنسّق في شكل “مشموم” جميل.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"2147897016839404914\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n      <div       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/282080.Guillaume_Musso">About Guillaume Musso</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/282080.Guillaume_Musso"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1487686506p3/282080.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer14849641431996673254">One of the most popular authors in France today. From his early childhood with reading books and plays, Guillaume Musso became convinced that one day, he too would write novels. After finishing high school in France, Guillaume Musso left for the United States at the age of 19. He spent several months in New York City, living with other young foreigners and earning his money by selling ice-cream. H</span>
  <span id="freeText14849641431996673254" style="display:none">One of the most popular authors in France today. From his early childhood with reading books and plays, Guillaume Musso became convinced that one day, he too would write novels. After finishing high school in France, Guillaume Musso left for the United States at the age of 19. He spent several months in New York City, living with other young foreigners and earning his money by selling ice-cream. He came home to France with his head filled with ideas for novels. The readers can easily see the influence his time in the United States has had on him, as the action in his books takes place overseas. He currently teaches in a high school in the south of France, all the while working on his novels. His first published novel was with Editions Anne Carriere in 2001: <i>Skidamarink</i>, this novel did not reach out to the masses however, but his following novels published on XO Editions have all been hugely successful, some of them translated into 20 languages. His novel, <i>Afterwards</i>, has been adapted to the big screen and was in cinemas January 2009, starring John Malkovich, Evangeline Lily and Romain Duris.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14849641431996673254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
